function rgpost(c){for(var a=0;a&lt;c.feed.entry.length;a++){for(var b=0;b&lt;c.feed.entry[a].link.length;b++)if("alternate"==c.feed.entry[a].link[b].rel){var e=c.feed.entry[a].link[b].href;break}b="thr$total"in c.feed.entry[a]?c.feed.entry[a].thr$total.$t+" Comments":"Comments";"1 Comments"==b&amp;&amp;(b="1 Comment");"0 Comments"==b&amp;&amp;(b="No Comments");var d=c.feed.entry[a].published.$t,h=d.substring(0,4),k=d.substring(5,7),d=d.substring(8,10),l=c.feed.entry[a].title.$t,g=c.feed.entry[a].category[0].term, f=c.feed.entry[a].media$thumbnail.url;-1!=f.indexOf("img.youtube.com")&amp;&amp;(f=c.feed.entry[a].media$thumbnail.url.replace("default","0"));b='&lt;li class="als-item"&gt;&lt;a href='+e+'&gt;&lt;img src="'+f.replace("/s72-c/","/s170-h110-c/")+'"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;div class="repostt"&gt;&lt;a href="/search/label/'+g+'?&amp;max-results=8"&gt;'+g+"&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3&gt;&lt;a href="+e+"&gt;"+l+'&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;font class="reposth2"&gt; '+[,"January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"][parseInt(k,10)]+" "+ d+", "+h+" / &lt;a href="+e+"#comments&gt;"+b+"&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;";document.write(b)}};

      //Recent Gallery Slider Post Widget By Label Part1
function rpslider(c){for(var a=0;a&lt;c.feed.entry.length;a++){for(var b=0;b&lt;c.feed.entry[a].link.length;b++)if("alternate"==c.feed.entry[a].link[b].rel){var f=c.feed.entry[a].link[b].href;break}b="thr$total"in c.feed.entry[a]?c.feed.entry[a].thr$total.$t+" Comments":"Comments";"1 Comments"==b&amp;&amp;(b="1 Comment");"0 Comments"==b&amp;&amp;(b="");var d=c.feed.entry[a].published.$t,h=d.substring(0,4),k=d.substring(5,7),d=d.substring(8,10),l=c.feed.entry[a].title.$t,g=c.feed.entry[a].category[0].term, e=c.feed.entry[a].media$thumbnail.url;-1!=e.indexOf("img.youtube.com")&amp;&amp;(e=c.feed.entry[a].media$thumbnail.url.replace("default","0"));b='&lt;li&gt;&lt;img src="'+e.replace("/s72-c/","/s753-h340-c/")+'" class="rpsimg"/&gt;&lt;div class="lof-main-item-desc"&gt;&lt;h3&gt;&lt;a href="/search/label/'+g+'?&amp;max-results=8"&gt;&lt;large&gt;'+g+"&lt;/large&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;i&gt; \u2014 "+[,"January","February","March","April","May","June","July","August","September","October","November","December"][parseInt(k,10)]+" "+d+", "+h+"  &lt;a href="+f+"#comments&gt;&lt;small&gt;"+ b+"&lt;/small&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;a href="+f+"&gt;"+l+"&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/li&gt;";document.write(b)}};

          <a name="4794474380747016020">
          </a>
          <article class="post hentry" id="4794474380747016020" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
           <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-4794474380747016020" itemprop="articleBody">
            <h2 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
             <a href="http://www.vitasumarte.com/2015/02/extra-fashion-fotomanzia-vol-2.html">
              Extra Fashion: Fotomanzia vol. 2
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="post_author_date date updated vcard">
             By
             <a href="#author-info" id="scrollTo">
              <font class="post_author">
               <span class="fn">
                Gloria Di Blasi
               </span>
              </font>
             </a>
             -
             <script>
              var lastDate = '09 feb 2015';
             </script>
             09 feb 2015
 -
            </div>
            Uff... non c' pace per questa generazione dallo scatto incondizionato: e la luce, l'angolatura, dall'alto s, dal basso no, speriamo che il meteo cambi che ho gi postato 3 foto di neve e 4 di pioggia, con trucco, senza trucco, coi filtri, #nofilter... un impegno senza tregua, pensiamo di aver fatto lo scatto perfetto e invece, dietro di noi... IL MALE.
            <br/>
            Non tutto il male vien per nuocere poich da tale fenomeno ne scaturisce uno nuovo di cui sto per depositare il brevetto: la
            <b>
             FOTOMANZIA
            </b>
            ,
            <span style="font-size: large;">
             il nostro destino svelato dagli
             <b>
              sfondi delle foto
             </b>
            </span>
            .
            <br/>
            Leggi anche tu il futuro osservando ci che c' dietro di te negli scatti della tua
            <b>
             beautiful vita quotidiana
            </b>
            .
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e23hXNLo0Bk/VNee8JogJWI/AAAAAAAAeWA/-NQ2Ih7LalE/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B00.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-e23hXNLo0Bk/VNee8JogJWI/AAAAAAAAeWA/-NQ2Ih7LalE/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B00.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Se nella tua foto  presente
             <b>
              un bidone colmo di cartone
             </b>
             ma mancano i sacchi neri,
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             tieniti pronta a reagire perch subirai un rifiuto parziale.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Vevcv9vVop8/VNee-Hxlw_I/AAAAAAAAeWI/Ew1TaW6S5_I/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B01.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Vevcv9vVop8/VNee-Hxlw_I/AAAAAAAAeWI/Ew1TaW6S5_I/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B01.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Un
             <b>
              uccello in agguato
             </b>
             fa rima con maglione cagato:  dunque presagio di sventura
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             e di bucato a mano o in lavatrice.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SW98LDJc_YQ/VNee_Abj5ZI/AAAAAAAAeWQ/TDj2gm9qyz4/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B02.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SW98LDJc_YQ/VNee_Abj5ZI/AAAAAAAAeWQ/TDj2gm9qyz4/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B02.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Se dietro di te c'
             <b>
              il ritratto di una figlia di Satana
             </b>
             , dovrai difenderti
             <br/>
             dalle femmine
             <i>
              soloinvidioSSe
             </i>
             che si fingeranno amiche solo per consigliarti abiti di merda.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1_B11AWUq78/VNefB0uS7sI/AAAAAAAAeWY/6xTdd7RejgE/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B02b.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1_B11AWUq78/VNefB0uS7sI/AAAAAAAAeWY/6xTdd7RejgE/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B02b.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Ti stai facendo un selfie quand'ecco che si materializza
             <b>
              lo spirito agitato di Vittorio Brumotti
             </b>
             ?
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Abbombazza! Infortunio sul lavoro, 100% Inail.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D8b4XSibmFM/VNefCyhpZzI/AAAAAAAAeWg/MAnflxBbtd4/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B03.jpeg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D8b4XSibmFM/VNefCyhpZzI/AAAAAAAAeWg/MAnflxBbtd4/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B03.jpeg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             Una
             <b>
              vettura abbinata ai colori improbabili del tuo maglione
             </b>
              un evento
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             tanto raro quanto fortunato: l'anima gemella vigila su di te.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b2BetlqLl10/VNefGX3E7kI/AAAAAAAAeWo/QyV8kLvW0ig/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B03b.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b2BetlqLl10/VNefGX3E7kI/AAAAAAAAeWo/QyV8kLvW0ig/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B03b.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <b>
              Una donna afro che nasconde il volto dietro a una borsa no logo
             </b>
             :
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             fai di tutto per mostrare il tuo lato migliore, il rischio di cadere nell'anonimato  vicino.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vdsFHwIxkAo/VNefH1B3WHI/AAAAAAAAeWw/7Tqa_CEjO-Y/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B04.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vdsFHwIxkAo/VNefH1B3WHI/AAAAAAAAeWw/7Tqa_CEjO-Y/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B04.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <b>
              Un tram in procinto di investirti
             </b>
              segno che la vita ti sottoporr ad una prova
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             che potrai superare solo se sprezzerai il pericolo con un casco.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xVq4xsmGir0/VNefI1jPB5I/AAAAAAAAeW4/CWh4df0CKow/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B06.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
              <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xVq4xsmGir0/VNefI1jPB5I/AAAAAAAAeW4/CWh4df0CKow/s1600/sullo%2Bsfondo%2Bphotobumper%2Bextra%2Bfashion%2Bstreet%2Bstyle%2Bvita%2Bsu%2Bmarte%2B06.jpg"/>
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <b>
              Donna dai capelli rossi impegnata in una post-produzione marrone
             </b>
             :
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             devi saper apprezzare tutte le sfumature che la vita di offre.
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
             <br/>
            </div>
            <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            </div>
            <br/>
            <div class="stw">

    var olderLink = $('a.older-link');

     newerLink.html('&lt;span&gt;'+$(data).find('.post h2.post-title').text()+'&lt;/span&gt;');   
    },"html");

    },"html");

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('#dtab').easyResponsiveTabs({
            type: 'accordion', //Types: default, vertical, accordion           
            width: 'auto', //auto or any width like 600px
            fit: true,   // 100% fit in a container
            closed: 'accordion', // Start closed if in accordion view
            activate: function(event) { // Callback function if tab is switched
                var $tab = $(this);
                var $info = $('#tabInfo');
                var $name = $('span', $info);

                $name.text($tab.text());

                $info.show();
            }
        });

        $('#htab').easyResponsiveTabs({
            type: 'default',
            width: 'auto',
            fit: true
        });

        $('#vtab').easyResponsiveTabs({
            type: 'vertical',
            width: 'auto',
            fit: true
        });

  <!-- Codice per accettazione cookie - Inizio -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[
(function(window) {
  if (!!window.cookieChoices) {
    return window.cookieChoices;
  }
  var document = window.document;  
  var supportsTextContent = 'textContent' in document.body;
  var cookieChoices = (function() {
    var cookieName = 'displayCookieConsent';
    var cookieConsentId = 'cookieChoiceInfo';
    var dismissLinkId = 'cookieChoiceDismiss';
    function _createHeaderElement(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref) {
      var butterBarStyles = 'position:fixed;width:100%;background-color:#eee;' +
          'margin:0; left:0; top:0;padding:4px;z-index:1000;text-align:center;';
      var cookieConsentElement = document.createElement('div');
      cookieConsentElement.id = cookieConsentId;
      cookieConsentElement.style.cssText = butterBarStyles;
      cookieConsentElement.appendChild(_createConsentText(cookieText));
      if (!!linkText &amp;&amp; !!linkHref) {
        cookieConsentElement.appendChild(_createInformationLink(linkText, linkHref));
      }
      cookieConsentElement.appendChild(_createDismissLink(dismissText));
      return cookieConsentElement;
    }
    function _createDialogElement(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref) {
      var glassStyle = 'position:fixed;width:100%;height:100%;z-index:999;' +
          'top:0;left:0;opacity:0.5;filter:alpha(opacity=50);' +
          'background-color:#ccc;';
      var dialogStyle = 'z-index:1000;position:fixed;left:50%;top:50%';
      var contentStyle = 'position:relative;left:-50%;margin-top:-25%;' +
          'background-color:#fff;padding:20px;box-shadow:4px 4px 25px #888;';
      var cookieConsentElement = document.createElement('div');
      cookieConsentElement.id = cookieConsentId;
      var glassPanel = document.createElement('div');
      glassPanel.style.cssText = glassStyle;
      var content = document.createElement('div');
      content.style.cssText = contentStyle;
      var dialog = document.createElement('div');
      dialog.style.cssText = dialogStyle;
      var dismissLink = _createDismissLink(dismissText);
      dismissLink.style.display = 'block';
      dismissLink.style.textAlign = 'right';
      dismissLink.style.marginTop = '8px';
      content.appendChild(_createConsentText(cookieText));
      if (!!linkText &amp;&amp; !!linkHref) {
        content.appendChild(_createInformationLink(linkText, linkHref));
      }
      content.appendChild(dismissLink);
      dialog.appendChild(content);
      cookieConsentElement.appendChild(glassPanel);
      cookieConsentElement.appendChild(dialog);
      return cookieConsentElement;
    }
    function _setElementText(element, text) {
      if (supportsTextContent) {
        element.textContent = text;
      } else {
        element.innerText = text;
      }
    }
    function _createConsentText(cookieText) {
      var consentText = document.createElement('span');
      _setElementText(consentText, cookieText);
      return consentText;
    }
    function _createDismissLink(dismissText) {
      var dismissLink = document.createElement('a');
      _setElementText(dismissLink, dismissText);
      dismissLink.id = dismissLinkId;
      dismissLink.href = '#';
      dismissLink.style.marginLeft = '24px';
      return dismissLink;
    }
    function _createInformationLink(linkText, linkHref) {
      var infoLink = document.createElement('a');
      _setElementText(infoLink, linkText);
      infoLink.href = linkHref;
      infoLink.target = '_blank';
      infoLink.style.marginLeft = '8px';
      return infoLink;
    }
    function _dismissLinkClick() {
      _saveUserPreference();
      _removeCookieConsent();
      return false;
    }
    function _showCookieConsent(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref, isDialog) {
      if (_shouldDisplayConsent()) {
        _removeCookieConsent();
        var consentElement = (isDialog) ?
            _createDialogElement(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref) :
            _createHeaderElement(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref);
        var fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
        fragment.appendChild(consentElement);
        document.body.appendChild(fragment.cloneNode(true));
        document.getElementById(dismissLinkId).onclick = _dismissLinkClick;
      }
    }
    function showCookieConsentBar(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref) {
      _showCookieConsent(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref, false);
    }
    function showCookieConsentDialog(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref) {
      _showCookieConsent(cookieText, dismissText, linkText, linkHref, true);
    }
    function _removeCookieConsent() {
      var cookieChoiceElement = document.getElementById(cookieConsentId);
      if (cookieChoiceElement != null) {
        cookieChoiceElement.parentNode.removeChild(cookieChoiceElement);
      }
    }
    function _saveUserPreference() {
// Durata del cookie di un anno
      var expiryDate = new Date();
      expiryDate.setFullYear(expiryDate.getFullYear() + 1);
      document.cookie = cookieName + '=y; expires=' + expiryDate.toGMTString();
    }
    function _shouldDisplayConsent() {
      // Per mostrare il banner solo in mancanza del cookie
      return !document.cookie.match(new RegExp(cookieName + '=([^;]+)'));
    }
    var exports = {};
    exports.showCookieConsentBar = showCookieConsentBar;
    exports.showCookieConsentDialog = showCookieConsentDialog;
    return exports;
  })();
  window.cookieChoices = cookieChoices;
  return cookieChoices;
})(this);
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(event) {
    cookieChoices.showCookieConsentBar('Questo blog usa cookies di terze parti per rendere migliore la navigazione agli utenti. Per saperne di pi cliccate su Info. Se continuate a navigare, senza bloccare i cookies, accettate il loro uso', 'ACCETTO', '+Info', 'http://www.vitasumarte.com/p/informativa-cookies.html');
  });
//]]&gt;
  </script>
  <!-- Codice per accettazione cookie - Fine -->
